 The comments chunaav ayog ne simbal order ke para 15 kaa zikr karte hue kaha he ki jiske paksh main vidhaayi or santhnik takat he, use hi asli daavedaar mana jaataa he
 The Commission has clearly stated in paragraphs 37, 38 and 39 of its order that no documents in support of Mulayam Singh Yadav were given, while the Commission gave them time till 9 January
 itnaa hi nahin, mulaayam singh yadav ne akhilesh yadav kii ore se jamaa kiye gaye shapathpatron kii satyata par to sawaal uthaae, lekin ayog ko apni aapatti ko lekar kabhi santusht nahin kiya
 The Commission has written in para 39 of its order that despite repeated opportunities neither Mulayam Singh Yadav gave any affidavit nor named any MP or MLA whose affidavit he deems to be fake
 ayog ne jo faisla sunaaya he, uske para 36 main vistaar se likhaa he ki akhilesh yadav ke group ne 228 main se 205 vidhayakon, 68 main se 56 emelsi or 24 main se 15 saansadon ke samarthan kii chitti di
 In addition, Akhilesh submitted affidavits of 28 out of 46 National Executive members and 4,400 out of 5,731 national representatives, stating that he was with Akhilesh's camp
 tippaniyan The Election Commission, referring to para 15 of the Symbol Order, has said that the one who has legislative and organizational strength in its favor is considered the real contender
 ayog ne apane order ke para 37, 38 or 39 main saaf likhaa he ki mulaayam singh yadav kii ore se samarthan main koi dastauez nahin die gaye, jabaki ayog ne unhen 9 janvari tak kaa vakt diya tha
 Not only this, Mulayam Singh Yadav questioned the veracity of the affidavits submitted by Akhilesh Yadav, but never satisfied his objection to the Commission
 ayog ne apane aadesh ke para 39 main likhaa he ki baar-baar avasar die jane ke baavjood na to mulaayam singh yadav ne koi halafanama diya or na hi kisi saansad yaa vidhayak kaa naam bataaya, jiske shapathpatr ko vah farzi maanate hon

 Following protests by students in protest against Banaras Hindu University (BHU) appointment of Professor Feroz Khan to the Sanskrit Sciences Religion Department, the professor has received support from AMU
 jahaan biechayu ke chaatr firoz ke muslim hone ke kaaran unki niyukti kaa virodh kar rahe hai, vahiin aligarh muslim uniwarsity (AMU) ke chaatr unke samarthan main aage aae hai
 In a letter to BHU, AMU alumni association president Salman Imtiaz said, "we are deeply saddened by Khan's public statement
 muslim hone ke kaaran virodh hone par biechayu main unhen apmaan mahasoos hota he
 "he said," We are with him and his ability
 agar unke saath kuch galat hua to ham shant nahin rahenge
 Their life, their freedom and security must be thought of first
 unhen sauhardrapurn vaataavaran main padhaane kaa mauka diya janaa chahie
 "the letter further reads," We condemn the insensitive behavior of students who believe that a Muslim cannot read or study Sanskrit at BHU
 yah sharmnaak he
 We urge you to teach these students of India's diversity, plurality, constitutional nature
 "chaatrasangh ke upaadhyaksh hamaja sughayan ne kaha, "professor ko ujisi ke niyamon ke anusaar niyukt kiya gaya tha or dharm ke aadhaar par unke saath bhedbhaav us vaataavaran kii maansikta dikhti he, jo in chaatro ne dikhaaya he
 " aswin ne aate hi ek hi over main vaan jill or fof du plasis ko pavilion kii raah dikhaa di
 He lbw to Jill on a personal score of 20, while du Plessis (0) was caught by Pujara
 aswin ne chot ke baad vaapasi kar rahe jepi dumini ko bhi zyada der nahin tikne diya or unhen 15 ran ke nijee score par slip main rahane ke haathon kaich kara diya
 Ravindra Jadeja walked Dean Elgar, AB de Villiers, Dan Vilas and Kagiso Rabada
 varun aaron ko ek wicket mila
 No single athlete can be considered the greatest in the world of sports, because different athletes are at their peak in different rounds and there is no comparison between them
 lekin usan bolt ne lagaataar shandaar pradarshan karke ek baar phir is bahes ko janm de diya he ki kya ve sabase mahaan athlete hai
 There is also a good reason for this to happen, if they look at their performance so far, then Bolt seems to be at the forefront of great athletes
 khel kii duniya main boxing ke lijend mohammad ali hon yaa phir footbal ke jaadugar pele
 
 
 
 yaa phir argentina ke super star deoga maradona hon yaa america basketbaal ke jeniyas maaikel jordan
 All these are the legend of the game world
 apane-apane khelon ke diggaj
 Now Usain Bolt has also joined this list
 aapke dhyaan main hoga hi ki ek baar mohammad ali ne khud hi kah diya tha- ai em greatest
 That means i am the greatest
 jab aap lagaataar behatar pradarshan karte hai to aisa ehsaas aa hi jaataa he
 Usain Bolt is also now where no one is seen around him
 ek athlete ke taur par bolt sabase khaas hai or unka andaaj bhi unhen dusron se bahut stylish bana detaa he
 It seems that he is a champion by health
 
 
 
 
 unka apane aap par aisa bharosa he jo unhen har mushkil main bhi champion banaata he
 He missed out on the 100m semi-finals at the recent Beijing World Championships, but knew that the final was going to be named after him
 unhone aisa kar dikhaaya
 Later he also said, "there was nothing special in it
 mujhe maaloom tha ki main dusron se behatar hum or mujhe khud par niyantran rakhkar daudna bhar tha
 " baharhaal bolt kii tulana karl louis se bhi kii ja rahi he, lekin bolt louis se behatar dikhaai pad rahe hai
 Carl Louis won 5 gold medals at the Olympics from 1984 to 1996, while he won the World Championship title 6 times
 duusari ore bolt ne mahaj 2 olympic khelon main 6 gold medal jite hai, vahiin world championships main bolt 11 baar baaji maar chuke hai
 Yes, it's a different thing to see if they stay on track like Louis for a long time
 lekin agar ve utane lambey samay tak bane rahe, to unki kamyaabiyon kaa graph kahaan pahonchega, ye dekhne vaali baat hogi
 Bolt has such dominance on the track that they start celebrating victory before reaching the finish line
 maujuuda samay main 100 meter or 200 meter daud kaa world ricard bolt ke naam he
 He is the first athlete to win 6 gold medals in an Olympic race and also the first athlete to win the 100 m and 200 m titles in two consecutive Olympic Games
 tippaniyan From Barack Obama to Prince Harry
 
 
 sabake sab bolt ke diwane hai
 His fans are present all over the world
 maaikel johnson to unhen beete 20 saalon main athlete kii duniya kaa global super star maanate hai
 Bolt has shown his dominance in the sports world
 aise main unako jamaica kaa sabase mahaan athlete mana jane laga he
 He is also being compared to Bob Marley, but Usain Bolt
 
 
 usan bolt hai
 
 
 
 jinhen racing trek par haraana naammumkin he
 But Usain Bolt has once again given rise to a debate about whether he is the greatest athlete
 aisa hone kii upyukt vajah bhi he, yadi unke ab tak ke pradarshan par najar daali jaae, to bolt mahaan athleton kii qatari main sabase aage najar aa rahe hai
 In the sports world, be it the boxing legend Mohammad Ali or the football wizard Pelé
 
 
 
 Or the Argentine superstar Dioga Maradona or the American basketball genius Michael Jordan
 ye sab khel kii duniya ke lijend hai
 Giants of their respective sports
 ab is suchi main usan bolt bhi shaamil ho gaye hai
 It will be in your attention that once Mohammad Ali himself said - i am the greatest
 yani sabase mahaan main hi hum
 When you consistently perform better, you realize it
 usan bolt bhi ab vahaan hai jahaan unke aasapaas koi nahin dikhataa
 As an athlete, Bolt is the most special and his style also makes him very stylish than others
 aisa maaloom hota he ki tabiyat se hi champion hai
 
 
 
 
 He has such confidence in himself that makes him a champion even in every difficulty
 haal hi main beijing world championships main 100 meter semifinal main ve chook gaye, lekin unhen maaloom tha ki final unke naam hone vaala he
 He did so
 baad main unhone kaha bhi, "isamen kuch khaas nahin tha
 i knew that i was better than others and i had to run to control myself
 " Although Bolt is also being compared to Carl Louis, but Bolt looks better than Louis
 karl louis ne 1984 se 1996 tak olympic main 5 gold medal jite the, jabaki unhone 6 baar world championships kaa khitaab jeeta tha
 On the other hand, Bolt has won 6 gold medals in just 2 Olympic Games, while Bolt has won 11 times in the World Championship
 haa, yah alag baat he ki ve louis kii tarah lambey samay tak trek par bane rahete hai yaa nahin yah dekhnaa hoga
 But if they remain for that long, then where will the graph of their successes reach, it will be a matter to be seen
 bolt kaa trek par aisa dabadabaa he ki ve finnish line tak pahunchane se pehle hi jeet kaa jashn manaanaa shuru kar dete hai
 At present, the world record of 100 meters and 200 meters race is named after Bolt
 olympic main daud main 6 gold medal jeetne vaale ve pehle athlete hai or lagaataar do olympic khelon main 100 meter or 200 meter kaa khitaab jeetne vaale bhi ve pehle athlete hai
